## Diagram 2

```mermaid
stateDiagram
    [*] --> CREATED
    CREATED --> INROUTE : depart/dispatch
    INROUTE --> DELIVERED : arrived/delivered
    INROUTE --> DELAYED : delay detected
    DELAYED --> INROUTE : resumed
    DELAYED --> DELIVERED : delivered after delay
    DELIVERED --> [*]
```
